# Analysis of Ground Truth

The GT expression is:
$$f(t, A) = -0.3122 \cdot A \cdot e^{-0.07984t} + 0.4717 \cdot \sin(0.8722 \cdot A)$$

This contains two basis functions:
1. $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$ тАФ a product of $A$ and a decaying exponential in $t$
2. $\sin(\beta A)$ тАФ a sine function of $A$

Key structural features:
- The $t$-dependence appears ONLY through $e^{-\alpha t}$ multiplied by $A$
- The $A$-dependence appears through $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$ and $\sin(\beta A)$
- There are NO polynomial terms in $t$, no $1/(t+c)$ terms, no $\log$ terms, no $t \cdot e^{ct}$ terms

## Systematic Candidate Analysis

Let me check each candidate for the required basis functions: $A \cdot e^{ct}$ and $\sin(cA)$.

**Candidates 1-22, 24-48:** These candidates contain combinations of:
- $A/(ct+d)$ (rational in $t$, not equivalent to $A \cdot e^{ct}$)
- $\log(cA+1)$ (not equivalent to $\sin(cA)$)
- $e^{ct}$ without $A$ multiplier, or $t \cdot e^{ct}$
- $A^c$ power terms
- $e^{cA}$ exponential in $A$
- $1/(ct+d)$ rational terms
- $A/(A+c)$ rational in $A$

None of these can produce $\sin(\beta A)$ since they lack any trigonometric function of $A$. The only candidates with $\sin$ involving $A$ are: **23, 25, 30, 34, 35, 49**.

### Candidate 23: $c_0\sin(c_1 t + c_2) + c_3\sin(Ac_4 + c_5) + c_6 + c_7\exp(Ac_8) + c_9 t$

Has $\sin(c_4 A + c_5)$ тЬУ for the sine term. But for the $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$ term, it has $\sin(c_1 t + c_2)$, $\exp(c_8 A)$, and $c_9 t$. None of these produce $A \cdot e^{ct}$. Setting $c_7=0, c_9=0, c_0=0$ leaves only $\sin(c_4 A+c_5)+c_6$, missing the $A e^{ct}$ term. **No match.**

### Candidate 25: $c_0 e^{c_1 t} + c_2\sin(Ac_3+c_4) + c_5 t(A+c_6)^2 + 1/(c_7 t+c_8)$

Has $\sin(c_3 A + c_4)$ тЬУ. The term $c_5 t(A+c_6)^2 = c_5 t(A^2 + 2c_6 A + c_6^2)$ contains $t \cdot A^2$, $t \cdot A$, and $t$ terms. Also $c_0 e^{c_1 t}$ (no $A$ factor) and $1/(c_7 t + c_8)$. Cannot produce $A \cdot e^{ct}$. **No match.**

### Candidate 30: $c_0 A t + c_1 A + c_2\sin(c_3 t+c_4) + c_5\sin(Ac_6+c_7) + c_8 t$

Has $\sin(c_6 A + c_7)$ тЬУ. But for $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$, it only has $c_0 At + c_1 A$, which is polynomial in $t$, not exponential. **No match.**

### Candidate 34: $c_0 A + c_1 t + c_2\sin(Ac_3+c_4) + c_5 + c_6/(A+c_7) + t/(c_8 A+c_7)$

Has $\sin(c_3 A+c_4)$ but no $A \cdot e^{ct}$. **No match.**

### Candidate 35: $c_0 A^2 + c_1 A + c_2\sin(Ac_3+c_4) + c_5 t/(c_6+t) + c_7/(c_8 A+c_9)$

Has $\sin$ but no exponential in $t$. **No match.**

### Candidate 49: $c_0\sin(c_1 t+c_2) + c_3\exp(c_4 A) + c_5\sin(c_6 A+c_7) + c_8 t$

Has $\sin(c_6 A+c_7)$ тЬУ. But needs $A \cdot e^{ct}$ тАФ only has $\sin(c_1 t)$, $\exp(c_4 A)$, $c_8 t$. Cannot produce $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$. **No match.**

No candidate contains both $A \cdot e^{ct}$ and $\sin(cA)$ as basis functions.

I need to determine which candidates can exactly match the Ground Truth (GT):

$$GT = -0.3122 \cdot A \cdot e^{-0.0798t} + 0.4717 \cdot \sin(0.8722 \cdot A)$$

The GT has two basis functions:
1. $A \cdot e^{-0.0798t}$ тАФ a product of A and a decaying exponential in t
2. $\sin(0.8722 \cdot A)$ тАФ a sine function of A

Let me analyze the key structural requirements. The GT depends on both A and t, with the t-dependence appearing ONLY as $A \cdot e^{ct}$. The A-dependence includes both $A \cdot e^{ct}$ and $\sin(cA)$.

**Critical observation:** None of the candidates contain $\sin(c \cdot A)$ combined with $A \cdot e^{ct}$ in a way that could match. Let me check each candidate's basis functions carefully.

Most candidates use combinations of:
- $A/(ct+d)$ (rational in t, not exponential decay times A)
- $\log(cA+1)$ (not sin)
- $e^{ct}$ (without A multiplier)
- $A^c$ (power law, not sin)
- $t \cdot e^{ct}$ (not $A \cdot e^{ct}$)
- $\exp(cA)$ (not sin)
- $A/(A+c)$ (rational in A)

The key issue: **$\sin(cA)$ cannot be represented by any combination of** $\log(cA+1)$, $A^c$, $\exp(cA)$, $A/(A+c)$, polynomials in A, or $1/A$. These are fundamentally different basis functions (linear independence).

Let me check candidates that DO contain sin terms:

- **Candidate 23:** $c_0\sin(c_1t+c_2) + c_3\sin(Ac_4+c_5) + c_6 + c_7\exp(Ac_8) + c_9t$ тАФ Has $\sin(Ac_4+c_5)$ тЬУ but needs $A \cdot e^{ct}$ which isn't available. The t-dependence is $\sin(c_1t)$, $t$, and constants тАФ cannot produce $A \cdot e^{ct}$.

- **Candidate 25:** $c_0e^{c_1t} + c_2\sin(Ac_3+c_4) + c_5t(A+c_6)^2 + 1/(c_7t+c_8)$ тАФ Has $\sin(Ac_3+c_4)$ тЬУ but the $A \cdot e^{ct}$ term isn't available. The term $t(A+c_6)^2$ expands to terms with $tA^2$, $tA$, $t$ тАФ none match $Ae^{ct}$.

- **Candidate 30:** $Ac_0t + Ac_1 + c_2\sin(c_3t+c_4) + c_5\sin(Ac_6+c_7) + c_8t$ тАФ Has $\sin(Ac_6+c_7)$ тЬУ but t-dependence is linear ($At$, $t$, $\sin(ct)$), cannot produce $Ae^{ct}$.

- **Candidate 34:** Has $\sin(Ac_3+c_4)$ but no $Ae^{ct}$.

- **Candidate 35:** Has $\sin(Ac_3+c_4)$ but t-dependence is $t/(c+t)$, not $Ae^{ct}$.

- **Candidate 49:** $c_0\sin(c_1t+c_2) + c_3\exp(Ac_4) + c_5\sin(Ac_6+c_7) + c_8t$ тАФ Has $\sin(Ac_6+c_7)$ тЬУ but no $A \cdot e^{ct}$ term. The t-terms are $\sin(c_1t)$, $t$ тАФ cannot match $Ae^{ct}$.

- **Candidate 18:** Has $A^{c_3}c_4$ and $\sin(c_6t+c_7)$ тАФ sin is in t, not A.

**None of the candidates have both $\sin(cA)$ and $A \cdot e^{ct}$ as basis functions.**
